WhErE iS lAp 4?
LEP5
So I did the math on how long it would take a player to reach the final lap count when Pepeevee busts into Pizzahead's room with 1262023 laps. For this I'm using my best times at John Gutter (since that's the level all the lap songs takes place in) by only grabbing Toppins that were in my way and nothing else. I'm also using how long it would take to complete subsequent laps by subtracting my best single lap time to my best non-P Rank lap 2 time. My best single lap time (not grabbing everything) is 1:36 My best non P-Rank lap 2 time is 2:26 Subtracting those 2 gives us 50 seconds for a completed second lap. Give or take a few seconds depending on any flub ups, but for the sake of the equations lets just go with 50 seconds for every lap after entering the portal. 50 x 1262021 (subtracting the first two laps since this is adding onto that time) gives us 63101050 seconds. Dividing that by 60 (cause 60 seconds in a minute) gives 1051684 minutes give or take a few milliseconds Dividng that by 60 again (cause 60 seconds in an hour) gives 17528 and some change hours Dividng that by 24 (24 hours in a day) gives 730 and some change days. Dividing that by 365 (365 days in a year) gives us 2 years. 2 years of non-stop gameplay with little to no mistakes, at least for me, I honestly couldn't be bothered to see what the current world records for John Gutter single lap and P-Rank were.

this rules
Absurdism is a philosophy proposing that the world is irrational and meaningless. The conflict between the human desire for order and fairness in a chaotic and uncaring world is known as "the absurd." To be an absurdist is not to lament the meaninglessness of the world, but to embrace it and define your own meaning. To find satisfaction and contentment in embracing the capricious nature of the universe.  Sisyphus was cursed by the gods to push a boulder up a hill for all eternity, Albert Camus, the father of Absurdism proposes that his ultimate act of rebellion would be to turn his punishment, into purpose, an eternal purpose. "The struggle itself towards the heights is enough to fill a man's heart. One must imagine Sisyphus happy."  We observe Peppino embracing fully the concept of the absurd, channeling the spirit of Sisyphus, willingly turning his punishment into paradise, finding meaning and purpose in the endless rolling of the boulder, or maybe rolling of the dough would be a more appropriate comparison.

I like the subtle lore RecD's been dropping in the main level music songs by showing Peppino's slow decent into madness.  In Pizza Time, he's freaking out over EVERYTHING, but is still primarily worried about the main plot: Pizza Face blowing up his restaurant.  In Deservioli, he's becoming more and more paranoid, but also determined to get a P RANK, no longer caring about the main mission and seeking the satisfaction of the purple P.  And now, in Lap 3, he's become so obsessed with the simple THRILL of the last two laps that he resorts to BREAKING REALITY ITSELF to gain said satisfaction for eternity. There it is. That's it. I've heard people speculate about how making Peppino a villain in a sequel (or whatever other form of media) following this game would be a great idea. But not knowing the motivation. There you go. Wrapped up in a little bow. The motivation is this balding middle aged Italian man in the middle of a mid life crisis becomes an increasingly unhinged adrenaline junkie whilst trying to save his restaurant.  Being a mere normal pizza chef isn't enough for him anymore. He can't take it, he starts having withdrawal for his life being in danger. He needs more. More adrenaline, more speed, more death, more enemies, more obstacles, he *has* to push the limits far beyond they were ever meant to be. Pizza Face has created a monster. And he now has to right his mistake, if only cause his life is in danger of Peppino gets any more unstable with his reality altering spices he puts into these special pizzas.  Like I said this could work for literally anything. A sequel game. A mod. A fanfic. A online comic! All of those would work! I just need to see someone use this idea! This is at the very least the perfect idea for an AU.
